msg:As a five-star hotel operator. I have to say that this hotel is the worst among all five-star hotels! Typical gold and jade, the outside is ruined and the inside is stained. The hotel operators put all their thoughts on decoration. From the first lesson when I walked into this hotel, whether it was the front desk, the restaurant or other places, the staff basically had no sense of service. When you come here, you are not a customer, but a fellow villager passing by from far away from their hometown. They won't provide you with quality service, they will only give you rules. The day of check-in was New Year's Eve, and the package included dinner. As a result, the front desk staff spoke vaguely about everything I asked him. There is only this sentence: You can't go to eat at 4:30, you can only wait until 7 o'clock." The reason is because the holiday buffet is already full, so we can only bear the second wave... At that time, everyone was confused! Who am I? Me Where? What was I doing? I finally found the manager on duty and was "allowed" to dine at 4:30 pm. But the truth is: from 4:30 pm to 8:30 pm, this restaurant was never full. .
I originally came to them to celebrate the New Year because their package included breakfast and dinner. As a result, what I ate was an ordinary buffet with no Chinese New Year a**osphere at all. The variety is not huge in a five-star hotel, but they are basically very cheap. It's just like eating a casual breakfast when staying in a star-rated hotel outside. After eating two meals, I felt like vomiting. The Chinese New Year buffet is so simple, I wonder what their usual buffet will be like.

I had to brush the faces of two adults when I checked in, but when I gave them toiletries, they only gave me a toothbrush!
The room is overall very old but has some modern facilities. There is a big gap with genuine five-star hotels. There is no smart toilet. The hair dryer is very difficult to use. The two aunties who are responsible for cleaning the guest room are pretty good.

Finally, let‚Äôs talk about the swimming pool. The water is the coldest among all five-star hotels. Total lack of consideration for customers. Basically, the changing rooms in all five-star hotels are filled with large and small clean white bath towels for customers to use for swimming. And their bath towels, which are not old but not old, are placed at the front desk. If you want to use it, you must press the room card. This measure is really disgusting! What do you consider your customers? ! Do you think of yours as a gym on the side of the road?
Ordinary swimming pool locker rooms will be equipped with: skin care products after swimming and bathing, cotton swabs. Basic necessities such as cotton pads, combs, hair dryers, and swimsuit dryers. And there are staff inside to provide timely services. But there are no staff in their dressing room, except for two hair dryers!
Even more disgusting. Even in the swimming pool of the gym on the side of the road, you can't see the sight of you swimming in the water. There was an uncle on the shore who took a garbage net and fished it back and forth in the water. It‚Äôs really frustrating!
I also read the reviews before coming here. It feels like I was deceived by false positive reviews. What benefits do those who praise someone by name gain? !
Also, when I made the reservation a month ago, I agreed that I could extend my stay when I arrived at the hotel, and I would not be sold after I arrived at the hotel. Said the buffet was fully booked. But if you want to pay a high price, buy it elsewhere. There is a place to sit. We can understand your desire to make a fortune during the Chinese New Year. But for a five-star hotel, your appearance is too ugly! Completely disregarding the feelings of customers, disregarding one's own credibility, not keeping promises, and only seeking profit! Fortunately, because the order was placed through the Ctrip platform, Ctrip's customer service staff tracked and communicated throughout the process. Although it was properly resolved in the end. But all in all, it is very unpleasant, especially on a special day like the Chinese New Year. It is really disappointing.
